<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports modal and non-modal modes</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Focus is trapped and scrolling is blocked in the modal mode</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Provides screen reader announcements via rendered title and description</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Pressing <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Esc</code> closes the dialog</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>To use the dialog component correctly, you&#x27;ll need to understand its anatomy and
how we name its parts.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>
</blockquote>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the dialog package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> dialog</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/dialog&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The dialog package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - Behavior logic for the dialog.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps behavior to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Pass a unique <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMachine</code> so generated element ids stay predictable.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:dialog/usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div data-scope="tabs" <h3 id="managing-focus-within-the-dialog" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Managing focus within the dialog<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#managing-focus-within-the-dialog"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the dialog opens, it focuses the first focusable element and keeps keyboard
focus inside the dialog.</p>
<p>To control what receives focus on open, pass <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">initialFocusEl</code>.</p>

<p>To control what receives focus when the dialog closes, pass <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">finalFocusEl</code>.</p>
<h3 id="dialog-vs-non-modal-dialog" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Dialog vs non-modal dialog<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#dialog-vs-non-modal-dialog"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">modal</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code> to allow interaction with content behind the dialog.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>dialog<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">modal</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="closing-the-dialog-on-interaction-outside" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Closing the dialog on interaction outside<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#closing-the-dialog-on-interaction-outside"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, the dialog closes when you click its overlay. You can set
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnInteractOutside</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code> if you want the modal to stay visible.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>dialog<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">closeOnInteractOutside</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>You can also customize the behavior by passing a function to the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onInteractOutside</code> callback and calling <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">event.preventDefault()</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>dialog<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onInteractOutside</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">event</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> target <span class="token operator">=</span> event<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">target</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token keyword control-flow">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>target<span class="token operator">?.</span><span class="token method function property-access">closest</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;&lt;selector&gt;&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">      <span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> event<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">preventDefault</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-open-state-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for open state changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-open-state-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the dialog is opened or closed, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code> callback is invoked.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>dialog<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onOpenChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { open: boolean }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;open:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">open</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="closing-with-escape" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Closing with Escape<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#closing-with-escape"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnEscape</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code> if the dialog should not close on <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Esc</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>dialog<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">closeOnEscape</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-dialog" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled dialog<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-dialog"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To control the dialog&#x27;s open state, pass the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code>
properties.</p>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>

<h3 id="controlling-the-scroll-behavior" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlling the scroll behavior<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlling-the-scroll-behavior"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the dialog is open, it prevents scrolling on the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">body</code> element. To disable
this behavior, set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">preventScroll</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>dialog<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">preventScroll</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="creating-an-alert-dialog" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Creating an alert dialog<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#creating-an-alert-dialog"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The dialog supports both <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dialog</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">alertdialog</code> roles. It uses <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dialog</code> by
default. Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">role</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">alertdialog</code> for urgent actions.</p>
<p>That&#x27;s it! Now you have an alert dialog.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>dialog<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">role</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;alertdialog&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>By definition, an alert dialog will contain two or more action buttons. We
recommend setting focus to the least destructive action via <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">initialFocusEl</code>.</p>
</blockquote>
<h3 id="labeling-without-a-visible-title" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Labeling without a visible title<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#labeling-without-a-visible-title"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>If you do not render a title element, provide <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">aria-label</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>dialog<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token string-property property">&quot;aria-label&quot;</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Delete project&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the backdrop element */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;positioner&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the positioner element */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the content element */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the close trigger element */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="open-and-closed-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Open and closed state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#open-and-closed-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The dialog has two states: <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closed</code>. You can use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-state</code>
attribute to style the dialog or trigger based on its state.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the open state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the open state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="nested-dialogs" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Nested dialogs<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#nested-dialogs"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When dialogs are nested (a dialog opened from within another dialog), the layer
stack automatically applies data attributes to help create visual hierarchy.</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-nested</code> - Applied to nested dialogs</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-has-nested</code> - Applied to dialogs that have nested dialogs open</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">--nested-layer-count</code> - CSS variable indicating the number of nested dialogs</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">/* Scale down parent dialogs when they have nested children */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-has-nested</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">transform</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token function">scale</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token function">calc</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span> <span class="token operator">-</span> <span class="token function">var</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token variable">--nested-layer-count</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">0.05</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">transition</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> transform <span class="token number">0.2</span><span class="token unit">s</span> ease-in-out<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">/* Style nested dialogs differently */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-nested</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">border</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token unit">px</span> solid <span class="token function">var</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token variable">--accent-color</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">/* Create depth effect using backdrop opacity */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;backdrop&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-has-nested</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">opacity</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token function">calc</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0.4</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token function">var</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token variable">--nested-layer-count</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">0.1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The dialog machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ trigger: string; positioner: string; backdrop: string; content: string; closeTrigger: string; title: string; description: string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the dialog. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">trapFocus</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to trap focus inside the dialog when it&#x27;s opened</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">preventScroll</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to prevent scrolling behind the dialog when it&#x27;s opened</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">modal</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to prevent pointer interaction outside the element and hide all content below it</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">initialFocusEl</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; HTMLElement</code><span class="d_block">Element to receive focus when the dialog is opened</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">finalFocusEl</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; HTMLElement</code><span class="d_block">Element to receive focus when the dialog is closed</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">restoreFocus</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to restore focus to the element that had focus before the dialog was opened</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnInteractOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to close the dialog when the outside is clicked</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnEscape</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to close the dialog when the escape key is pressed</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">aria-label</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">Human readable label for the dialog, in event the dialog title is not rendered</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">role</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;dialog&quot; | &quot;alertdialog&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The dialog&#x27;s role</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The controlled open state of the dialog</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultOpen</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The initial open state of the dialog when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the open state of the dialog.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: OpenChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to call when the dialog&#x27;s open state changes</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; Node | ShadowRoot | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onEscapeKeyDown</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: KeyboardEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the escape key is pressed</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onRequestDismiss</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: LayerDismissEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when this layer is closed due to a parent layer being closed</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPointerDownOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: PointerDownOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the pointer is pressed down outside the component</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFocusOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: FocusOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the focus is moved outside the component</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onInteractOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: InteractOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when an interaction happens outside the component</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">persistentElements</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(() =&gt; Element)[]</code><span class="d_block">Returns the persistent elements that:
- should not have pointer-events disabled
- should not trigger the dismiss event</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The dialog <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the dialog is open</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setOpen</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(open: boolean) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to open or close the dialog</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="data-attributes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Data Attributes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#data-attributes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Trigger</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_4 max-w_lg"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-scope</kbd></div><span>dialog</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-part</kbd></div><span>trigger</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-state</kbd></div><span>&quot;open&quot; | &quot;closed&quot;</span></div></div></div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Backdrop</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_4 max-w_lg"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-scope</kbd></div><span>dialog</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-part</kbd></div><span>backdrop</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-state</kbd></div><span>&quot;open&quot; | &quot;closed&quot;</span></div></div></div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Content</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_4 max-w_lg"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-scope</kbd></div><span>dialog</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-part</kbd></div><span>content</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-state</kbd></div><span>&quot;open&quot; | &quot;closed&quot;</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-nested</kbd></div><span>dialog</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-has-nested</kbd></div><span>dialog</span></div></div></div></div>
<h3 id="css-variables" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">CSS Variables<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#css-variables"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Content</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_4 max-w_lg"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">--layer-index</kbd></div><span>The index of the dismissable in the layer stack</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">--nested-layer-count</kbd></div><span>The number of nested dialogs</span></div></div></div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Backdrop</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_4 max-w_lg"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">--layer-index</kbd></div><span>The index of the dismissable in the layer stack</span></div></div></div></div>
<h2 id="accessibility" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Accessibility<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Adheres to the
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/alertdialog" class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px">Alert and Message Dialogs WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-interactions" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Keyboard Interactions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keyboard-interactions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Enter</kbd></div><div>When focus is on the trigger, opens the dialog.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Tab</kbd></div><div>Moves focus to the next focusable element within the content. Focus is trapped within the dialog.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Shift + Tab</kbd></div><div>Moves focus to the previous focusable element. Focus is trapped within the dialog.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Esc</kbd></div><div>Closes the dialog and moves focus to trigger or the defined final focus element</div></li></ul><a href="https://github.com/chakra-ui/zag/edit/main/website/data/components/dialog.mdx" class="d_inline-flex ai_center gap_1 textStyle_a fs_sm mt_14"><svg dialog is a window overlaid on either the primary window or another dialog\nwindow. Content behind a modal dialog is inert, meaning that users cannot\ninteract with it.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cresources pkg=\"@zag-js/dialog\"\u003e\n\u003cshowcase id=\"Dialog\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFeatures\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports modal and non-modal modes\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFocus is trapped and scrolling is blocked in the modal mode\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eProvides screen reader announcements via rendered title and description\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePressing \u003ccode\u003eEsc\u003c/code\u003e closes the dialog\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eInstallation\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eInstall the dialog package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"dialog/installation.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eAnatomy\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo use the dialog component correctly, you'll need to understand its anatomy and\nhow we name its parts.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach part includes a \u003ccode\u003edata-part\u003c/code\u003e attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003canatomy id=\"dialog\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsage\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eImport the dialog package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as dialog from \"@zag-js/dialog\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe dialog package exports two key functions:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - Behavior logic for the dialog.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps behavior to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePass a unique \u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003euseMachine\u003c/code\u003e so generated element ids stay predictable.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"dialog/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eManaging focus within the dialog\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the dialog opens, it focuses the first focusable element and keeps keyboard\nfocus inside the dialog.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo control what receives focus on open, pass \u003ccode\u003einitialFocusEl\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"dialog/initial-focus.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo control what receives focus when the dialog closes, pass \u003ccode\u003efinalFocusEl\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eDialog vs non-modal dialog\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003emodal\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e to allow interaction with content behind the dialog.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(dialog.machine, {\n  modal: false,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eClosing the dialog on interaction outside\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the dialog closes when you click its overlay. You can set\n\u003ccode\u003ecloseOnInteractOutside\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e if you want the modal to stay visible.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(dialog.machine, {\n  closeOnInteractOutside: false,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can also customize the behavior by passing a function to the\n\u003ccode\u003eonInteractOutside\u003c/code\u003e callback and calling \u003ccode\u003eevent.preventDefault()\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-7}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(dialog.machine, {\n  onInteractOutside(event) {\n    const target = event.target\n    if (target?.closest(\"\u0026#x3C;selector\u003e\")) {\n      return event.preventDefault()\n    }\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening for open state changes\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the dialog is opened or closed, the \u003ccode\u003eonOpenChange\u003c/code\u003e callback is invoked.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-7}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(dialog.machine, {\n  onOpenChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { open: boolean }\n    console.log(\"open:\", details.open)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eClosing with Escape\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003ecloseOnEscape\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e if the dialog should not close on \u003ccode\u003eEsc\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(dialog.machine, {\n  closeOnEscape: false,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlled dialog\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo control the dialog's open state, pass the \u003ccode\u003eopen\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonOpenChange\u003c/code\u003e\nproperties.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"dialog/controlled.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlling the scroll behavior\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the dialog is open, it prevents scrolling on the \u003ccode\u003ebody\u003c/code\u003e element. To disable\nthis behavior, set \u003ccode\u003epreventScroll\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(dialog.machine, {\n  preventScroll: false,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eCreating an alert dialog\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe dialog supports both \u003ccode\u003edialog\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003ealertdialog\u003c/code\u003e roles. It uses \u003ccode\u003edialog\u003c/code\u003e by\ndefault. Set \u003ccode\u003erole\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003ealertdialog\u003c/code\u003e for urgent actions.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThat's it! window or another dialog\nwindow. Content behind a modal dialog is inert, meaning that users cannot\ninteract with it.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/dialog\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"Dialog\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Supports modal and non-modal modes\n- Focus is trapped and scrolling is blocked in the modal mode\n- Provides screen reader announcements via rendered title and description\n- Pressing `Esc` closes the dialog\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the dialog package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"dialog/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nTo use the dialog component correctly, you'll need to understand its anatomy and\nhow we name its parts.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"dialog\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the dialog package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as dialog from \"@zag-js/dialog\"\n```\n\nThe dialog package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - Behavior logic for the dialog.\n- `connect` - Maps behavior to JSX props and event handlers.\n\n\u003e Pass a unique `id` to `useMachine` so generated element ids stay predictable.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"dialog/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Managing focus within the dialog\n\nWhen the dialog opens, it focuses the first focusable element and keeps keyboard\nfocus inside the dialog.\n\nTo control what receives focus on open, pass `initialFocusEl`.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"dialog/initial-focus.mdx\" /\u003e\n\nTo control what receives focus when the dialog closes, pass `finalFocusEl`.\n\n### Dialog vs non-modal dialog\n\nSet `modal` to `false` to allow interaction with content behind the dialog.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(dialog.machine, {\n  modal: false,\n})\n```\n\n### Closing the dialog on interaction outside\n\nBy default, the dialog closes when you click its overlay. You can set\n`closeOnInteractOutside` to `false` if you want the modal to stay visible.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(dialog.machine, {\n  closeOnInteractOutside: false,\n})\n```\n\nYou can also customize the behavior by passing a function to the\n`onInteractOutside` callback and calling `event.preventDefault()`.\n\n```jsx {2-7}\nconst service = useMachine(dialog.machine, {\n  onInteractOutside(event) {\n    const target = event.target\n    if (target?.closest(\"\u003cselector\u003e\")) {\n      return event.preventDefault()\n    }\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for open state changes\n\nWhen the dialog is opened or closed, the `onOpenChange` callback is invoked.\n\n```jsx {2-7}\nconst service = useMachine(dialog.machine, {\n  onOpenChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { open: boolean }\n    console.log(\"open:\", details.open)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Closing with Escape\n\nSet `closeOnEscape` to `false` if the dialog should not close on `Esc`.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(dialog.machine, {\n  closeOnEscape: false,\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled dialog\n\nTo control the dialog's open state, pass the `open` and `onOpenChange`\nproperties.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"dialog/controlled.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Controlling the scroll behavior\n\nWhen the dialog is open, it prevents scrolling on the `body` element. To disable\nthis behavior, set `preventScroll` to `false`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(dialog.machine, {\n  preventScroll: false,\n})\n```\n\n### Creating an alert dialog\n\nThe dialog supports both `dialog` and `alertdialog` roles. It uses `dialog` by\ndefault. Set `role` to `alertdialog` for urgent actions.\n\nThat's it! Now you have an alert dialog.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(dialog.machine, {\n  role: \"alertdialog\",\n})\n```\n\n\u003e By definition, an alert dialog will contain two or more action buttons. We\n\u003e recommend setting focus to the least destructive action via `initialFocusEl`.\n\n### Labeling without a visible title\n\nIf you do not render a title element, provide `aria-label`.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(dialog.machine, {\n  \"aria-label\": \"Delete project\",\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"trigger\"] {\n  /* styles for the trigger element */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"backdrop\"] {\n  /* styles for the backdrop element */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"positioner\"] {\n  /* styles for the positioner element */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"content\"] {\n  /* styles for the content element */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"title\"] {\n  /* styles for the title element */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"description\"] {\n  /* styles for the description element */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"close-trigger\"] {\n  /* styles for the close trigger element */\n}\n```\n\n### Open and closed state\n\nThe dialog has two states: `open` and `closed`. You can use the `data-state`\nattribute to style the dialog or trigger based on its state.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for the open state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for the open state */\n}\n```\n\n### Nested dialogs\n\nWhen dialogs are nested (a dialog opened from within another dialog), the layer\nstack automatically applies data attributes to help create visual hierarchy.\n\n- `data-nested` - Applied to nested dialogs\n- `data-has-nested` - Applied to dialogs that have nested dialogs open\n- `--nested-layer-count` - CSS variable indicating the number of nested dialogs\n\n```css\n/* Scale down parent dialogs when they have nested children */\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-has-nested] {\n  transform: scale(calc(1 - var(--nested-layer-count) * 0.05));\n  transition: transform 0.2s ease-in-out;\n}\n\n/* Style nested dialogs differently */\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-nested] {\n  border: 2px solid var(--accent-color);\n}\n\n/* Create depth effect using backdrop opacity */\n[data-part=\"backdrop\"][data-has-nested] {\n  opacity: calc(0.4 + var(--nested-layer-count) * 0.1);\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe dialog machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"dialog\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe dialog `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"dialog\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"dialog\" /\u003e\n\n### CSS Variables\n\n\u003cCssVarTable name=\"dialog\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\nAdheres to the\n[Alert and Message Dialogs WAI-ARIA design pattern](https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/alertdialog).\n\n### Keyboard Interactions\n\n\u003cKeyboardTable name=\"dialog\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Dialog\",\"description\":\"Using the dialog machine in your
